NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, Srinivasan, S., was born as a male child to Sundareson, C.K. on 16th July 1976, residing at No. 3e, Indra Gandhi
Street, Kallukuttai, Perungudi, Chennai-600 096. After an elaborate sexual reassignment Surgery, I have been living as
a female (Refference Dr. V. Jayaraman, M.S., M.Ch., MNAMS, Dip. N.B., Ph.D., FICS) Proffessor and Head Department
of Burns, Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010. The through clinical
Examination under Dr. V. Jayaraman shows that I could be treated as a female. Hence Srinivasan, S. shall be known as
Kowsalya, S.

Chennai,
26th June 2012.

S. SRINIVASAN.
